ptacr.SIFT_myTax_2021_Deductions

/*Identify number of records from previousweek*/
SEL
		Claim_Label
		,Count(*) AS Record_count_Previous
		,Sum(item_amnt) AS Item_Amnt
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
GROUP BY 1
ORDER BY 1
;

DROP TABLE ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19;

CREATE MULTISET VOLATILE TABLE uayca_2021_text_D01 AS (

SELECT
		Clnt_Intrnl_Id
		,TFN
		,Late_Form_tx_Id
		,Idv_Ocptn_Cd AS Idv_Ocptn_Cd
		,Trim(RegExp_Replace(Cr_Expns_Descn_Txt  , '[\s]+',' '))AS  Cr_Expns_Descn_Txt
		,Cr_Expns_Totl_Amt AS Cr_Expns_Totl_Amt
		,Form_Ln_Itm_Rept_Seq_Num
		,Orig_Ldg_Channel
FROM 	ptacr.SIFT_myTax_2021_Deductions

WHERE	(
			Cr_Expns_Descn_Txt  IS NOT NULL
			OR 
			Cr_Expns_Totl_Amt > 0.00
		)
/*
KY Notes: Change Primary Index
--) WITH DATA PRIMARY INDEX (Clnt_Intrnl_Id) ON COMMIT PRESERVE ROWS ;
*/
) WITH DATA 
PRIMARY INDEX (Clnt_Intrnl_Id, Form_Ln_Itm_Rept_Seq_Num) 
ON COMMIT PRESERVE ROWS ;

CREATE MULTISET VOLATILE TABLE uayca_2021_text_D05 AS (

SEL
		Clnt_Intrnl_Id
		,TFN
		,Late_Form_tx_Id
		,Idv_Ocptn_Cd AS Idv_Ocptn_Cd
		,Trim(RegExp_Replace(WRE_Othr_Expns_Descn_Txt  , '[\s]+',' '))AS  WRE_Othr_Expns_Descn_Txt
		,WRE_Othr_Expns_Totl_Amt AS WRE_Othr_Expns_Totl_Amt
		,Form_Ln_Itm_Rept_Seq_Num
		,Orig_Ldg_Channel
FROM 	ptacr.SIFT_myTax_2021_Deductions
WHERE
		(
		WRE_Othr_Expns_Descn_Txt  IS NOT NULL
		OR WRE_Othr_Expns_Totl_Amt > 0.00
		)
/*
KY Notes: Change Primary Index
--) WITH DATA PRIMARY INDEX (Clnt_Intrnl_Id) ON COMMIT PRESERVE ROWS ;
*/
) WITH DATA 
PRIMARY INDEX (Clnt_Intrnl_Id, Form_Ln_Itm_Rept_Seq_Num) 
ON COMMIT PRESERVE ROWS ;

INSERT INTO ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19

SEL
TFN
,'2021' AS Incm_Yr
,Idv_Ocptn_Cd AS Idv_Ocptn_Cd
, 'D05' AS Claim_Label

DROP TABLE uayca_2021_text_D01 ;

/*Identify number of records from current week*/
SEL
		Claim_Label
		,Count(*) AS Record_count_Current
		,Sum(item_amnt) AS Item_Amnt
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
GROUP BY 1
ORDER BY 1
;



SEL
		Claim_Label
		,Count(*) AS Record_count_Current
		/*
		KY Notes: Not require to Trim(RegExp_Replace( Category , '[\s]+',' ') as this was already done on the base table
		--,CASE WHEN Category LIKE '%TBA%' THEN 'TBA' ELSE Trim(RegExp_Replace( Category , '[\s]+',' ')) end AS Category
		*/
		,CASE WHEN Category LIKE '%TBA%' THEN 'TBA' ELSE Category end AS Category
		,Sum(item_amnt) AS Item_Amnt
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
GROUP BY 1,3
ORDER BY 1
;




SEL
		Claim_Label
		,Count(*) AS Record_count_Current
		/*
		KY Notes: Not require as the category has no spaces
		,Trim(RegExp_Replace( Category , '[\s]+',' ')) AS  Category
		*/
		,Category
		,Sum(item_amnt) AS Item_Amnt
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
WHERE	Category LIKE '%TBA%'
GROUP BY 1,3
ORDER BY 2 DESC, 4 DESC
;


SEL
		tfn
		,Claim_Label
		
		/*
		KY Notes: Not require to as this was already done on the base table
		--,Trim(RegExp_Replace( Descn_Txt  , '[\s]+',' ')) AS  Descn_Txt 
		--,Trim(RegExp_Replace( Category , '[\s]+',' ')) AS  Category
		*/				
		,Descn_Txt
		,Category
		
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
SAMPLE 5000
--group by 1,2,3,4

;

SEL
		Count(*) AS Record_count_Current
		,Descn_Txt
		,Sum(item_amnt) AS Item_Amnt
		,Category
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
WHERE	Category NOT LIKE '%TBA%'
GROUP BY 2,4
HAVING Record_count_Current > 10
ORDER BY 1 DESC, 1 DESC
;


SEL
		TFN
		,Incm_Yr
		,Idv_Ocptn_Cd
		,Claim_Label
		,Item_Amnt 
		,Form_Ln_Itm_Rept_Seq_Num
		,Orig_Ldg_Channel 
		/*
		KY Notes: Not require to as this was already done on the base table
		--,Trim(RegExp_Replace( Descn_Txt  , '[\s]+',' ')) AS  Descn_Txt 
		--,Trim(RegExp_Replace( Category , '[\s]+',' ')) AS  Category
		*/				
		,Descn_Txt
		,Category
		
FROM	ptim.uayca_text_2021_v19
WHERE	Item_Amnt > 10000.00
AND 	Category LIKE '%TBA%'

--group by 1,2,3,4
;
